if(font=="Italic"){
    nl = "@"
    conf = "p1:a,p2:$,p3_Height:4,p4_Height_nd:3,p5_maxLinLen:10,p6_defSmuMod:0,p7_numComm:3"
    if ((charNumber==0) || (character=="!")){ oneChar="// @$$ @   @"; };
    if ((charNumber==1) || (character==""")){ oneChar="      @_|_|_ @-|-|- @"; };
    if ((charNumber==2) || (character=="#")){ oneChar=" ||_ @(||$ @_||) @"; };
    if ((charNumber==3) || (character=="$")){ oneChar="   @0/ @/0 @"; };
    if ((charNumber==4) || (character=="%")){ oneChar="    @()/ @(X  @"; };

    if ((charNumber==0) || (character=="!")){ oneChar=""; };
    if ((charNumber==1) || (character==""")){ oneChar="~\@"; };
    if ((charNumber==2) || (character=="#")){ oneChar="\|/@"; };
    if ((charNumber==3) || (character=="$")){ oneChar="$|$@"; };
    if ((charNumber==4) || (character=="%")){ oneChar="$@"; };
    if ((charNumber==5) || (character=="&")){ oneChar="$$@"; };
    if ((charNumber==6) || (character=="'")){ oneChar="$@"; };
    if ((charNumber==7) || (character=="(")){ oneChar="$/@"; };
    if ((charNumber==8) || (character==")")){ oneChar="/\@"; };
    if ((charNumber==9) || (character=="*")){ oneChar="'|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==10) || (character=="+")){ oneChar="~)@"; };
    if ((charNumber==11) || (character==",")){ oneChar="~/@"; };
    if ((charNumber==12) || (character=="-")){ oneChar="/|$@"; };
    if ((charNumber==13) || (character==".")){ oneChar="|~@"; };
    if ((charNumber==14) || (character=="/")){ oneChar=" / @"; };
    if ((charNumber==15) || (character=="0")){ oneChar="~/@"; };
    if ((charNumber==16) || (character=="1")){ oneChar="(~)@"; };
    if ((charNumber==17) || (character=="2")){ oneChar="(~|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==18) || (character=="3")){ oneChar="o@"; };
    if ((charNumber==19) || (character=="4")){ oneChar="o@"; };

    if ((charNumber==22) || (character=="7")){ oneChar="\@"; };

    if ((charNumber==25) || (character==":")){ oneChar="|~|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==26) || (character==";")){ oneChar="|~)@"; };
    if ((charNumber==27) || (character=="<")){ oneChar="|~@"; };
    if ((charNumber==28) || (character=="=")){ oneChar="|~\@"; };
    if ((charNumber==29) || (character==">")){ oneChar="[~@"; };
    if ((charNumber==30) || (character=="?")){ oneChar="|~@"; };
    if ((charNumber==31) || (character=="@")){ oneChar="|~_@"; };
    if ((charNumber==32) || (character=="A")){ oneChar="|_|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==33) || (character=="B")){ oneChar="|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==34) || (character=="C")){ oneChar="$|@"; };
    if ((charNumber==35) || (character=="D")){ oneChar="|/@"; };
